description: Доступ к футбольным, автоспортивным, букмекерским и справочным данным Sportmonks
---

import { BlockInfoCard } from "@/components/ui/block-info-card"

<BlockInfoCard 
  type="sportmonks"
  color="#171534"
/>

## Инструкции по использованию

Интегрируйте the Sportmonks sports data APIs в рабочий процесс from a single block. Football: fixtures, livescores, leagues, seasons, stages, rounds, teams, squads, players, coaches, referees, venues, standings, topscorers, transfers, schedules, commentaries, TV stations, rivals, expected goals (xG), and predictions. Motorsport: sessions, drivers, teams, championship standings, laps, and pitstops. Odds: pre-match and in-play odds, bookmakers, and markets. Core: continents, countries, regions, cities, types, and time zones.



## Действия

### `sportmonks_football_expected_by_player`

Получение lineup-level expected goals (xG) values per player from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, fixture;player;team;type\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `expected` | array | Array of player-level expected goals \(xG\) entries |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the expected value |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the value |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player related to the value |
|   ↳ `team_id` | number | Team related to the value |
|   ↳ `lineup_id` | number | Lineup record the player relates to |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the expected value |
|   ↳ `data` | object | The expected value payload |
|     ↳ `value` | number | The xG value |

### `sportmonks_football_expected_by_team`

Получение fixture-level expected goals (xG) values per team from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, fixture;participant;type\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `expected` | array | Array of team-level expected goals \(xG\) entries |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the expected value |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the value |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the expected value |
|   ↳ `participant_id` | number | Team related to the expected value |
|   ↳ `data` | object | The expected value payload |
|     ↳ `value` | number | The xG value |
|   ↳ `location` | string | Home or away |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_commentaries`

Получение all textual commentaries available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, fixture;player\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `commentaries` | array | Array of commentary entries |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the commentary |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the commentary |
|   ↳ `comment` | string | The commentary text |
|   ↳ `minute` | number | Match minute of the comment |
|   ↳ `extra_minute` | number | Extra \(injury\) minute of the comment |
|   ↳ `is_goal` | boolean | Указывает,  comment is a goal |
|   ↳ `is_important` | boolean | Указывает,  comment is important |
|   ↳ `order` | number | Order of the comment |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_fixtures`

Получение all football fixtures available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participants;scores\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, fixtureLeagues:501\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of fixture objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_players`

Получение all football players available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, nationality;position\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order players by id \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `players` | array | Array of player objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the player |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the player |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the player |
|   ↳ `city_id` | number | City of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position of the player |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position of the player |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the player |
|   ↳ `common_name` | string | Name the player is known for |
|   ↳ `firstname` | string | First name of the player |
|   ↳ `lastname` | string | Last name of the player |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the player |
|   ↳ `display_name` | string | Display name of the player |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the player headshot |
|   ↳ `height` | number | Height of the player in cm |
|   ↳ `weight` | number | Weight of the player in kg |
|   ↳ `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the player |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_rivals`

Получение all teams with their rivals information from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, team;rival\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `rivals` | array | Array of rival relationships |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the rival |
|   ↳ `team_id` | number | Team the rivalry belongs to |
|   ↳ `rival_id` | number | Rival team id |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_teams`

Получение all football teams available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;venue\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order teams by id \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `teams` | array | Array of team objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the team |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the team |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of the team |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Home venue of the team |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the team |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the team |
|   ↳ `short_code` | string | Short code of the team |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the team logo |
|   ↳ `founded` | number | Founding year of the team |
|   ↳ `type` | string | Type of the team |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  team is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `last_played_at` | string | Date and time of the last played match |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_transfer_rumours`

Получение all transfer rumours available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;fromTeam;toTeam\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `transferRumours` | array | Array of transfer rumour objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the transfer rumour |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the transfer rumour |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player the rumour relates to |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position id of the player |
|   ↳ `from_team_id` | number | Team the player would transfer from |
|   ↳ `to_team_id` | number | Team the player would transfer to |
|   ↳ `transfer_fee_id` | number | Transfer fee id of the rumour |
|   ↳ `probability` | string | Probability of the rumour (например, LOW\) |
|   ↳ `source_name` | string | Name of the source of the rumour |
|   ↳ `source_url` | string | URL of the source of the rumour |
|   ↳ `amount` | number | Estimated transfer fee amount |
|   ↳ `currency` | string | Currency of the amount |
|   ↳ `date` | string | Date of the rumour |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the transfer rumour |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_transfers`

Получение all transfers available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;fromTeam;toTeam\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, transferTypes:219,220\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `transfers` | array | Array of transfer objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the transfer |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player who transferred |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the transfer |
|   ↳ `from_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred from |
|   ↳ `to_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred to |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `date` | string | Date of the transfer |
|   ↳ `career_ended` | boolean | Указывает,  transfer ended the career |
|   ↳ `completed` | boolean | Указывает,  transfer is completed |
|   ↳ `amount` | number | Transfer fee amount |

### `sportmonks_football_get_brackets_by_season`

Получение the knockout-stage tournament bracket (stages and progression edges) for a season ID

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `seasonId` | string | Да | The unique id of the season |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `brackets` | json | Bracket object containing stages \(fixtures grouped by knockout round\) and edges \(progression paths between fixtures\) |

### `sportmonks_football_get_coach`

Получение a single football coach by their ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `coachId` | string | Да | The unique id of the coach |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;teams;statistics\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `coach` | object | The requested coach object |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the coach |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player related to the coach |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the coach |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of the coach |
|   ↳ `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the coach |
|   ↳ `city_id` | number | Birth city of the coach |
|   ↳ `common_name` | string | Common name of the coach |
|   ↳ `firstname` | string | First name of the coach |
|   ↳ `lastname` | string | Last name of the coach |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the coach |
|   ↳ `display_name` | string | Display name of the coach |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the coach headshot |
|   ↳ `height` | number | Height of the coach in cm |
|   ↳ `weight` | number | Weight of the coach in kg |
|   ↳ `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the coach |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the coach |

### `sportmonks_football_get_coaches`

Получение all football coaches available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;teams\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, coachCountries:462\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `coaches` | array | Array of coach objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the coach |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player related to the coach |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the coach |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of the coach |
|   ↳ `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the coach |
|   ↳ `city_id` | number | Birth city of the coach |
|   ↳ `common_name` | string | Common name of the coach |
|   ↳ `firstname` | string | First name of the coach |
|   ↳ `lastname` | string | Last name of the coach |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the coach |
|   ↳ `display_name` | string | Display name of the coach |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the coach headshot |
|   ↳ `height` | number | Height of the coach in cm |
|   ↳ `weight` | number | Weight of the coach in kg |
|   ↳ `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the coach |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the coach |

### `sportmonks_football_get_coaches_by_country`

Получение all coaches for a country ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `countryId` | string | Да | The unique id of the country |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;nationality\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `coaches` | array | Array of coach objects for the country |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the coach |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player related to the coach |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the coach |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of the coach |
|   ↳ `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the coach |
|   ↳ `city_id` | number | Birth city of the coach |
|   ↳ `common_name` | string | Common name of the coach |
|   ↳ `firstname` | string | First name of the coach |
|   ↳ `lastname` | string | Last name of the coach |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the coach |
|   ↳ `display_name` | string | Display name of the coach |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the coach headshot |
|   ↳ `height` | number | Height of the coach in cm |
|   ↳ `weight` | number | Weight of the coach in kg |
|   ↳ `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the coach |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the coach |

### `sportmonks_football_get_commentaries_by_fixture`

Получение textual commentary for a fixture by fixture ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `fixtureId` | string | Да | The unique id of the fixture |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;relatedPlayer\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `commentaries` | array | Array of commentary entries for the fixture |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the commentary |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the commentary |
|   ↳ `comment` | string | The commentary text |
|   ↳ `minute` | number | Match minute of the comment |
|   ↳ `extra_minute` | number | Extra \(injury\) minute of the comment |
|   ↳ `is_goal` | boolean | Указывает,  comment is a goal |
|   ↳ `is_important` | boolean | Указывает,  comment is important |
|   ↳ `order` | number | Order of the comment |

### `sportmonks_football_get_current_leagues_by_team`

Получение all current leagues for a team ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `teamId` | string | Да | The unique id of the team |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;currentSeason\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order leagues \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `leagues` | array | Array of current league objects for the team |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the league |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the league |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of the league |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the league |
|   ↳ `active` | number | Указывает,  league is active \(1\) or inactive \(0\) |
|   ↳ `short_code` | string | Short code of the league |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the league logo |
|   ↳ `type` | string | Type of the league |
|   ↳ `sub_type` | string | Subtype of the league |
|   ↳ `last_played_at` | string | Date the last fixture was played |
|   ↳ `category` | number | Importance category of the league \(1-4\) |

### `sportmonks_football_get_expected_lineups_by_player`

Получение the premium expected lineups for a player ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `playerId` | string | Да | The unique id of the player |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;fixture\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `expectedLineups` | array | Array of expected lineup entries for the player |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the expected lineup record |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the expected lineup |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the expected lineup relates to |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player in the expected lineup |
|   ↳ `team_id` | number | Team of the expected lineup player |
|   ↳ `formation_field` | string | Formation field of the player |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position id of the player |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position id of the player |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the expected lineup record |
|   ↳ `formation_position` | number | Position of the player in the formation |
|   ↳ `player_name` | string | Name of the player |
|   ↳ `jersey_number` | number | Jersey number of the player |

### `sportmonks_football_get_expected_lineups_by_team`

Получение the premium expected lineups for a team ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `teamId` | string | Да | The unique id of the team |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;fixture\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `expectedLineups` | array | Array of expected lineup entries for the team |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the expected lineup record |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the expected lineup |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the expected lineup relates to |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player in the expected lineup |
|   ↳ `team_id` | number | Team of the expected lineup player |
|   ↳ `formation_field` | string | Formation field of the player |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position id of the player |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position id of the player |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the expected lineup record |
|   ↳ `formation_position` | number | Position of the player in the formation |
|   ↳ `player_name` | string | Name of the player |
|   ↳ `jersey_number` | number | Jersey number of the player |

### `sportmonks_football_get_extended_team_squad`

Получение all squad entries for a team (based on current seasons) by team ID

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `teamId` | string | Да | The unique id of the team |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;position\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `squad` | array | Array of extended squad entries for the team |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the squad record |
|   ↳ `transfer_id` | number | Transfer id of the squad record |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player in the squad |
|   ↳ `team_id` | number | Team of the squad |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position of the player in the squad |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position of the player in the squad |
|   ↳ `jersey_number` | number | Jersey number of the player |
|   ↳ `start` | string | Start contract date of the player |
|   ↳ `end` | string | End contract date of the player |

### `sportmonks_football_get_fixture`

Получение a single football fixture by its ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `fixtureId` | string | Да | The unique id of the fixture |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participants;scores;events;lineups;statistics\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, eventTypes:14\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixture` | object | The requested fixture object |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_fixtures_by_date`

Получение all football fixtures on a specific date (YYYY-MM-DD) from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `date` | string | Да | The date to fetch fixtures for, in YYYY-MM-DD format |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participants;scores;league\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, fixtureLeagues:501,271\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order fixtures by starting_at \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of fixture objects for the requested date |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_fixtures_by_date_range`

Получение football fixtures between two dates (YYYY-MM-DD) from Sportmonks. Max range is 100 days.

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `startDate` | string | Да | Start date in YYYY-MM-DD format |
| `endDate` | string | Да | End date in YYYY-MM-DD format \(max 100 days after start\) |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participants;scores\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, fixtureLeagues:501,271\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order fixtures by starting_at \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of fixture objects within the requested date range |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_grouped_standings_by_round`

Получение the standing table for a round ID grouped by group where applicable from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `roundId` | string | Да | The unique id of the round |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participant;details\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, standingGroups:246697\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `standings` | json | Standings for the round: an array of groups \(each with id, name and a standings array\) when groups exist, otherwise a flat array of standing entries |

### `sportmonks_football_get_head_to_head`

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |

| `team2` | string | Да | The id of the second team |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participants;scores\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order fixtures by starting_at \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of head-to-head fixture objects between the two teams |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_latest_coaches`

Получение all coaches that have received updates in the past two hours

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;nationality\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `coaches` | array | Array of recently updated coach objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the coach |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player related to the coach |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the coach |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of the coach |
|   ↳ `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the coach |
|   ↳ `city_id` | number | Birth city of the coach |
|   ↳ `common_name` | string | Common name of the coach |
|   ↳ `firstname` | string | First name of the coach |
|   ↳ `lastname` | string | Last name of the coach |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the coach |
|   ↳ `display_name` | string | Display name of the coach |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the coach headshot |
|   ↳ `height` | number | Height of the coach in cm |
|   ↳ `weight` | number | Weight of the coach in kg |
|   ↳ `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the coach |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the coach |

| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, nationality;position\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `players` | array | Array of recently updated player objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the player |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the player |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the player |
|   ↳ `city_id` | number | City of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position of the player |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position of the player |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the player |
|   ↳ `common_name` | string | Name the player is known for |
|   ↳ `firstname` | string | First name of the player |
|   ↳ `lastname` | string | Last name of the player |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the player |
|   ↳ `display_name` | string | Display name of the player |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the player headshot |
|   ↳ `height` | number | Height of the player in cm |
|   ↳ `weight` | number | Weight of the player in kg |
|   ↳ `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the player |

### `sportmonks_football_get_latest_totw`

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `leagueId` | string | Да | The unique id of the league |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, fixture;team;player;round\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `totw` | array | Array of the latest Team of the Week entries for the league |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the TOTW entry |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player of the team of the week |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the TOTW player played in |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `team_id` | number | Team the TOTW player played for |
|   ↳ `rating` | string | Rating of the TOTW player |
|   ↳ `formation_position` | number | Player position in the TOTW formation |
|   ↳ `formation` | string | The TOTW's formation |

### `sportmonks_football_get_latest_transfers`

Получение the latest transfers available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;fromTeam;toTeam\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, transferTypes:219,220\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `transfers` | array | Array of the latest transfer objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the transfer |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player who transferred |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the transfer |
|   ↳ `from_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred from |
|   ↳ `to_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred to |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `date` | string | Date of the transfer |
|   ↳ `career_ended` | boolean | Указывает,  transfer ended the career |
|   ↳ `completed` | boolean | Указывает,  transfer is completed |
|   ↳ `amount` | number | Transfer fee amount |

### `sportmonks_football_get_league`

Получение a single football league by its ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `leagueId` | string | Да | The unique id of the league |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;currentSeason;seasons\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `league` | object | The requested league object |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the league |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the league |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of the league |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the league |
|   ↳ `active` | number | Указывает,  league is active \(1\) or inactive \(0\) |
|   ↳ `short_code` | string | Short code of the league |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the league logo |
|   ↳ `type` | string | Type of the league |
|   ↳ `sub_type` | string | Subtype of the league |
|   ↳ `last_played_at` | string | Date the last fixture was played |
|   ↳ `category` | number | Importance category of the league \(1-4\) |

### `sportmonks_football_get_live_probabilities`

Получение all live (in-play) prediction probabilities from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, type;fixture\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `predictions` | array | Array of live probability prediction objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the live prediction record |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the prediction belongs to |
|   ↳ `period_id` | number | Match period the prediction was recorded in |
|   ↳ `minute` | number | Match minute the prediction was generated |
|   ↳ `predictions` | json | Home win, away win and draw probabilities as percentages |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the prediction \(237 for fulltime result\) |

### `sportmonks_football_get_livescores`

Получение fixtures starting within 15 minutes and currently in progress from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participants;scores;events\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, fixtureLeagues:501\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of live fixture objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_match_facts`

Получение all available match facts within your Sportmonks subscription (beta)

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, type;sport;fixture\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, matchFactTypes:76088\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `matchFacts` | array | Array of match fact objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the match fact |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the match fact |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the match fact |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the match fact |
|   ↳ `participant` | string | Team the fact relates to \(home or away\) |
|   ↳ `basis` | string | Basis of the match fact (например, h2h, overall\) |
|   ↳ `data` | json | Match fact data payload \(counts and percentages\) |
|   ↳ `natural_language` | string | Human-readable description of the match fact |
|   ↳ `category` | string | Category of the match fact |
|   ↳ `scope` | string | Scope of the match fact |

| `matchFacts` | array | Array of match fact objects for the league |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the match fact |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the match fact |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the match fact |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the match fact |
|   ↳ `participant` | string | Team the fact relates to \(home or away\) |
|   ↳ `basis` | string | Basis of the match fact (например, h2h, overall\) |
|   ↳ `data` | json | Match fact data payload \(counts and percentages\) |
|   ↳ `natural_language` | string | Human-readable description of the match fact |
|   ↳ `category` | string | Category of the match fact |
|   ↳ `scope` | string | Scope of the match fact |

### `sportmonks_football_get_past_fixtures_by_tv_station`

Получение all past fixtures that were available for a TV station ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `tvStationId` | string | Да | The unique id of the TV station |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participants\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, fixtureLeagues:501\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of past fixture objects for the TV station |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_player`

Получение a single football player by their ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `playerId` | string | Да | The unique id of the player |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;position;teams.team;statistics\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `player` | object | The requested player object |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the player |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the player |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the player |
|   ↳ `city_id` | number | City of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position of the player |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position of the player |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the player |
|   ↳ `common_name` | string | Name the player is known for |
|   ↳ `firstname` | string | First name of the player |
|   ↳ `lastname` | string | Last name of the player |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the player |
|   ↳ `display_name` | string | Display name of the player |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the player headshot |
|   ↳ `height` | number | Height of the player in cm |
|   ↳ `weight` | number | Weight of the player in kg |
|   ↳ `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the player |

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |

| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, newsitemLeagues:8\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order news by id \(asc or desc\) |

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `news` | array | Array of post-match news articles |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the news article |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the news article |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League related to the news article |
|   ↳ `title` | string | Title of the news article |
|   ↳ `type` | string | Type of the news \(prematch or postmatch\) |

| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |

| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, predictionTypes:236\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `predictions` | array | Array of prediction probability objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the prediction |

|   ↳ `predictions` | json | Prediction payload \(varies by type: score map, value bet object, etc.\) |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the prediction |

### `sportmonks_football_get_round`

Получение a single football round by its ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `roundId` | string | Да | The unique id of the round |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, league;season;stage;fixtures\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `round` | object | The requested round object |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the round |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the round |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League of the round |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season of the round |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage of the round |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the round |
|   ↳ `finished` | boolean | Указывает,  round is finished |
|   ↳ `is_current` | boolean | Указывает,  round is the current round |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Start date of the round |
|   ↳ `ending_at` | string | End date of the round |
|   ↳ `games_in_current_week` | boolean | Указывает,  round has fixtures this week |

| `roundId` | string | Да | The unique id of the round |

| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, seasonstatisticTypes:52,88\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |

|   ↳ `value` | json | Statistic value payload \(varies by type\) |

### `sportmonks_football_get_season`

Получение a single football season by its ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `seasonId` | string | Да | The unique id of the season |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, league;stages;fixtures\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `season` | object | The requested season object |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the season |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the season |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League of the season |
|   ↳ `tie_breaker_rule_id` | number | Tie-breaker rule of the season |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the season (например, 2023/2024\) |
|   ↳ `finished` | boolean | Указывает,  season is finished |
|   ↳ `pending` | boolean | Указывает,  season is pending |
|   ↳ `is_current` | boolean | Указывает,  season is the current season |
|   ↳ `standing_method` | string | Standing calculation method |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Start date of the season |
|   ↳ `ending_at` | string | End date of the season |
|   ↳ `standings_recalculated_at` | string | Last standings recalculation time |
|   ↳ `games_in_current_week` | boolean | Указывает,  season has fixtures this week |

|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group related to the correction |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the correction |
|   ↳ `value` | number | Amount of points awarded or deducted |
|   ↳ `calc_type` | string | Calculation type applied (например, + or -\) |
|   ↳ `participant_type` | string | Type of the participant (например, team\) |
|   ↳ `participant_id` | number | Participant the correction applies to |
|   ↳ `active` | boolean | Указывает,  correction is active |

| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `team` | object | The requested team object |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the team |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the team |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of the team |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Home venue of the team |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the team |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the team |
|   ↳ `short_code` | string | Short code of the team |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the team logo |
|   ↳ `founded` | number | Founding year of the team |
|   ↳ `type` | string | Type of the team |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  team is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `last_played_at` | string | Date and time of the last played match |

### `sportmonks_football_get_team_rankings`

Получение all team rankings available within your Sportmonks subscription (beta)

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, team\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `teamRankings` | array | Array of team ranking objects |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the team ranking |
|   ↳ `team_id` | number | Team related to the ranking |
|   ↳ `date` | string | Date of the ranking |
|   ↳ `current_rank` | number | Placement of the team on that date |
|   ↳ `scaled_score` | number | Scaled score of the team \(0-100\) |

### `sportmonks_football_get_team_squad`

| --------- | ---- | ----------- |

|   ↳ `end` | string | End contract date of the player |

### `sportmonks_football_get_topscorers_by_season`

Получение the topscorers (goals, assists, cards) for a season by season ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `seasonId` | string | Да | The unique id of the season |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;participant;type\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, seasontopscorerTypes:208\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order topscorers by position \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `topscorers` | array | Array of topscorer entries for the season |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the topscorer record |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season related to the topscorer \(absent on stage topscorers\) |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League related to the topscorer |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage related to the topscorer |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player related to the topscorer |
|   ↳ `participant_id` | number | Team related to the topscorer |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the topscorer \(goals, assists, cards\) |
|   ↳ `position` | number | Position of the topscorer |
|   ↳ `total` | number | Number of goals, assists or cards |

| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |

|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the topscorer record |

|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League related to the topscorer |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage related to the topscorer |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player related to the topscorer |

### `sportmonks_football_get_totw`

Получение all available Team of the Week (TOTW) entries from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, fixture;team;player;round\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `totw` | array | Array of Team of the Week entries |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the TOTW entry |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player of the team of the week |
|   ↳ `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the TOTW player played in |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `team_id` | number | Team the TOTW player played for |
|   ↳ `rating` | string | Rating of the TOTW player |
|   ↳ `formation_position` | number | Player position in the TOTW formation |
|   ↳ `formation` | string | The TOTW's formation |

| `roundId` | string | Да | The unique id of the round |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |

| `totw` | array | Array of Team of the Week entries for the round |

|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played at |

|   ↳ `formation_position` | number | Player position in the TOTW formation |
|   ↳ `formation` | string | The TOTW's formation |

### `sportmonks_football_get_transfer`

Получение a single transfer by its ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `transferId` | string | Да | The unique id of the transfer |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;fromTeam;toTeam\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `transfer` | object | The requested transfer object |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the transfer |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player who transferred |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the transfer |
|   ↳ `from_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred from |
|   ↳ `to_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred to |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `date` | string | Date of the transfer |
|   ↳ `career_ended` | boolean | Указывает,  transfer ended the career |
|   ↳ `completed` | boolean | Указывает,  transfer is completed |
|   ↳ `amount` | number | Transfer fee amount |

### `sportmonks_football_get_transfer_rumour`

Получение a single transfer rumour by its ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `rumourId` | string | Да | The unique id of the transfer rumour |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;fromTeam;toTeam\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `transferRumour` | object | The requested transfer rumour object |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the transfer rumour |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the transfer rumour |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player the rumour relates to |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position id of the player |
|   ↳ `from_team_id` | number | Team the player would transfer from |
|   ↳ `to_team_id` | number | Team the player would transfer to |
|   ↳ `transfer_fee_id` | number | Transfer fee id of the rumour |
|   ↳ `probability` | string | Probability of the rumour (например, LOW\) |
|   ↳ `source_name` | string | Name of the source of the rumour |
|   ↳ `source_url` | string | URL of the source of the rumour |
|   ↳ `amount` | number | Estimated transfer fee amount |
|   ↳ `currency` | string | Currency of the amount |
|   ↳ `date` | string | Date of the rumour |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the transfer rumour |

### `sportmonks_football_get_transfers_between_dates`

Получение transfers within a date range (YYYY-MM-DD) from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `startDate` | string | Да | Start date in YYYY-MM-DD format |
| `endDate` | string | Да | End date in YYYY-MM-DD format |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, player;fromTeam;toTeam\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, transferTypes:219,220\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `transfers` | array | Array of transfer objects within the date range |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the transfer |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player who transferred |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the transfer |
|   ↳ `from_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred from |
|   ↳ `to_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred to |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position id of the transfer |
|   ↳ `date` | string | Date of the transfer |
|   ↳ `career_ended` | boolean | Указывает,  transfer ended the career |
|   ↳ `completed` | boolean | Указывает,  transfer is completed |
|   ↳ `amount` | number | Transfer fee amount |

### `sportmonks_football_get_upcoming_fixtures_by_market`

Получение all upcoming fixtures for a market ID from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `marketId` | string | Да | The unique id of the market |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participants;odds\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, fixtureLeagues:501\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of upcoming fixture objects for the market |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_search_coaches`

Search for football coaches by name from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `query` | string | Да | The coach name to search for (например, Gerrard\) |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;teams\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `coaches` | array | Array of coach objects matching the search query |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the coach |
|   ↳ `player_id` | number | Player related to the coach |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the coach |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of the coach |
|   ↳ `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the coach |
|   ↳ `city_id` | number | Birth city of the coach |
|   ↳ `common_name` | string | Common name of the coach |
|   ↳ `firstname` | string | First name of the coach |
|   ↳ `lastname` | string | Last name of the coach |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the coach |
|   ↳ `display_name` | string | Display name of the coach |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the coach headshot |
|   ↳ `height` | number | Height of the coach in cm |
|   ↳ `weight` | number | Weight of the coach in kg |
|   ↳ `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the coach |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the coach |

### `sportmonks_football_search_fixtures`

Search for football fixtures by name (participants) from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `query` | string | Да | The fixture name to search for (например, Celtic\) |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, participants;scores\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply (например, fixtureLeagues:501\) |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order fixtures by starting_at \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of fixture objects matching the search query |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   ↳ `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   ↳ `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   ↳ `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   ↳ `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   ↳ `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture (например, 1/1\) |
|   ↳ `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   ↳ `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   ↳ `placeholder` | boolean | Указывает,  fixture is a placeholder |
|   ↳ `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   ↳ `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   ↳ `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `query` | string | Да | The league name to search for (например, Premier\) |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;currentSeason\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order leagues \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `leagues` | array | Array of league objects matching the search query |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the league |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the league |

|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the league |
|   ↳ `active` | number | Указывает,  league is active \(1\) or inactive \(0\) |
|   ↳ `short_code` | string | Short code of the league |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the league logo |
|   ↳ `type` | string | Type of the league |
|   ↳ `sub_type` | string | Subtype of the league |
|   ↳ `last_played_at` | string | Date the last fixture was played |
|   ↳ `category` | number | Importance category of the league \(1-4\) |

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `query` | string | Да | The player name to search for (например, Tavernier\) |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, country;position;teams.team\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order players by id \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `players` | array | Array of player objects matching the search query |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the player |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the player |
|   ↳ `country_id` | number | Country of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the player |
|   ↳ `city_id` | number | City of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `position_id` | number | Position of the player |
|   ↳ `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position of the player |
|   ↳ `type_id` | number | Type of the player |
|   ↳ `common_name` | string | Name the player is known for |
|   ↳ `firstname` | string | First name of the player |
|   ↳ `lastname` | string | Last name of the player |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the player |
|   ↳ `display_name` | string | Display name of the player |
|   ↳ `image_path` | string | URL to the player headshot |
|   ↳ `height` | number | Height of the player in cm |
|   ↳ `weight` | number | Weight of the player in kg |
|   ↳ `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the player |
|   ↳ `gender` | string | Gender of the player |

### `sportmonks_football_search_rounds`

Search for football rounds by name from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `query` | string | Да | The round name to search for (например, 5\) |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, league;season\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `rounds` | array | Array of round objects matching the search query |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the round |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the round |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League of the round |
|   ↳ `season_id` | number | Season of the round |
|   ↳ `stage_id` | number | Stage of the round |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the round |
|   ↳ `finished` | boolean | Указывает,  round is finished |
|   ↳ `is_current` | boolean | Указывает,  round is the current round |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Start date of the round |
|   ↳ `ending_at` | string | End date of the round |
|   ↳ `games_in_current_week` | boolean | Указывает,  round has fixtures this week |

### `sportmonks_football_search_seasons`

Search for football seasons by name from Sportmonks

#### Вход

| Параметр | Тип | Обязательный | Описание |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
| `query` | string | Да | The season name to search for (например, 2023/2024\) |
| `include` | string | Нет | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response (например, league\) |
| `filters` | string | Нет | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | Нет | Number of results per page \(max 50, по умолчанию 25\) |
| `page` | string | Нет | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | Нет | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Выход

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `seasons` | array | Array of season objects matching the search query |
|   ↳ `id` | number | Unique id of the season |
|   ↳ `sport_id` | number | Sport of the season |
|   ↳ `league_id` | number | League of the season |
|   ↳ `tie_breaker_rule_id` | number | Tie-breaker rule of the season |
|   ↳ `name` | string | Name of the season (например, 2023/2024\) |
|   ↳ `finished` | boolean | Указывает,  season is finished |
|   ↳ `pending` | boolean | Указывает,  season is pending |
|   ↳ `is_current` | boolean | Указывает,  season is the current season |
|   ↳ `standing_method` | string | Standing calculation method |
|   ↳ `starting_at` | string | Start date of the season |
|   ↳ `ending_at` | string | End date of the season |
|   ↳ `standings_recalculated_at` | string | Last standings recalculation time |
|   ↳ `games_in_current_week` | boolean | Указывает,  season has fixtures this week |

| `apiKey` | string | Да | Sportmonks API token |
